***нервный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвный</a> (1615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>нерв</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nerv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nérvnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нервне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нервне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nerve; nervous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nérvnaja</b> klétka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nerve</b> cell</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nérvnaja sistéma</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nervous</b> system</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>nervous, easily excitable or provoked
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотрудник.html>сотру́дник</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оказаться.html>оказа́лся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвным</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молоды́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парень.html>па́рнем</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nóvyj sotrúdnik okazálsja <b>nérvnym</b> molodým párnem.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The new employee was a <b>nervous</b> young man.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>nerve-wracking, creating a lot of worry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nérvnaja</b> rabóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nerve-wracking</b> work</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***нереальность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льность</a> (29637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальный.html>нереа́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nereálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nereálʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>unreality</li>
<li>infeasibility, impracticability</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерешительный.html>нереши́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nerešítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерешительность.html>нереши́тельность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerešítelʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерешительность.html>нереши́тельности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерешительность.html>нереши́тельности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерешительность.html>нереши́тельностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>indecision, irresolution</li>
<li>hesitation, wavering, hesitancy, hesitance</li>

<li>dither</li>
<li>shilly-shally</li>
<li>half-heartedness</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неровный.html>неро́вный</a> (8006)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неровный.html>неро́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neróvnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерушимый.html>неруши́мый</a> (18231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушить.html>ру́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rúšitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to break</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерушимый.html>неруши́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerušímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unbreakable, inviolable, indissoluble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нерушимый.html>неруши́мый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>сою́з</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nerušímyj</b> sojúz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">unbreakable union</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нерушимый.html>неруши́мые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nerušímyje</b> svjázi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">indestructible ties</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***неряха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a> (31251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ря́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjáxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">snappy dresser</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerjáxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> messy, unkempt person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>шла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чером</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:попасться.html>попа́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лице</a> семикла́ссник <a href = vnd.unilang:костя.html>ко́стя</a> оре́шкин — нескла́день <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tepérʹ že, kogdá šlá oná opjátʹ véčerom, popálsja na úlice semiklássnik Kóstja Oréškin — neskládenʹ i <b>nerjáxa</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Now, as she was walking down the street again in the evening, she bumped into a seventh-grader, Kostya Oreshkin  — an awkward and <b>unkempt</b> boy.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лик.html>ли́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скручивать.html>скру́чивала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:редька.html>ре́дькой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:макушка.html>маку́шке</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>ре́дька</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сползать.html>сполза́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грызть.html>гры́зла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноготь.html>но́гти</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чулок.html>чулки́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:плохо.html>пло́хо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:натянутый.html>натя́нутые</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:морщиться.html>мо́рщились</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гармоника.html>гармо́никой</a> из-под <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совсем.html>совсе́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:длинный.html>дли́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:юбка.html>ю́бки</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Líka bylá jedvá li ne prósto <b>nerjáxa</b>, vólosy skrúčivala rédʹkoj na makúške, i to rédʹka vsegdá spolzála na bok; oná grýzla nógti, i čulkí u nejó, plóxo natjánutyje, mórščilisʹ garmónikoj iz-pod ne sovsém ješčó dlínnoj júbki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Lika was perhaps just a <b>messy</b> woman, her hair was tied on top with a radish, and the radish always slanted sideways; she had a habit of biting nails and her stockings were worn loosely, crumpled like accordions under her skirt that was not long enough at all.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***неряшливый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неряшливый.html>неря́шливый</a> (15873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nerjáxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slob</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ря́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjáxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dandy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, shortening of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ряжо́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjažóxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dandy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рядиться.html>ряди́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjadítʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dress up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряд</a></i> <span </p>

***несбыточный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несбыточный.html>несбы́точный</a> (20501)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сбы́точный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbýtočnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несбыточный.html>несбы́точный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesbýtočnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)несбы́точнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)несбы́точней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>unworkable, impracticable, infeasible</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несвежий.html>несве́жий</a> (17295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свежий.html>све́жий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svéžij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несвежий.html>несве́жий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesvéžij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stale</li>
<li>stagnant <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of air or water</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> already familiar, not new; outdated</li>
<li>in long use</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несвобода.html>несвобо́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesvobóda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несвобода.html>несвобо́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несвобода.html>несвобо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несвобода.html>несвобо́д</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несвоевременный.html>несвоевре́менный</a> (30768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:своевременный.html>своевре́менный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svojevrémennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несвоевременный.html>несвоевре́менный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesvojevrémennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>untimely, inopportune</li>
<li>late, tardy</li></ol>

***несение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ние</a> (31240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>carrying out, performance, execution; fulfilment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязанность.html>обя́занностей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nesénije</b> objázannostej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">performance of duties</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воинский.html>во́инской</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жбы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nesénije</b> vóinskoj slúžby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">carrying out of the military service</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***несколько.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́сколько</a> (1149)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skólʹko</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Не— There is no + <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> —amount, 'many' = There is no specific amount.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́сколько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néskolʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>somewhat, slightly, rather; some
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́сколько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удивленный.html>удивлён</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On byl <b>néskolʹko</b> udivljón</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He was rather surprised.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>multiple, a couple</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>a few, several, some (+ genitive)
